<rate>4</rate>< Review>
Typical Target store - all the stuff you would expect at this chain. I particularly like to grab stuff in their grocery section. You can get good deals on boxed foods, and there‚Äôs some decent produce. Love the furniture and some of the women‚Äôs clothes (I like A New Day and Xhilaration brands); baby clothes in here are so cute! There‚Äôs also a good selection of make-up and toiletries. There‚Äôs a CVS Pharmacy, Cafe and Starbucks inside as well. The employees seem a little rough around the edges lol but overall a clean well organized store. Driving to this complex can be a little tricky. Be safe when coming in and out as it‚Äôs right near the freeway. PS there‚Äôs a Tesla charging station in this complex.</Review>

I brought my dog back to do the bloodwork and the Doctor told us to keep him on medication and we did. A few weeks later our dog had trouble breathing and we decided to take him to another animal hospital (Bodhi animal hospital) they requested the medical records from Pacific pet hospital right away and they didn't send them, in the mean time they asked us what medication he was on and what Pacific pet hospital had said. <Response>{'time': 1582305869512, 'text': "Hi Essa. My name is Osama and I am one of the owners at Tahini. Thank you for your review and feedback. We are constantly working to improve our food and hearing back from customers helps us do so. First, I am glad to hear that you enjoyed your food. I do apologize that you felt the portion wasn't enough. We do our best to make sure every rice bowl, salad, and pita sandwich receive the same amount of meat. We do use a larger bowl because we do add your choice of veggies (lettuce, tomatoes, red onions, pickled cucumbers, regular cucumbers, pickled turnips, parsley mix, olives, bell peppers, and pepperoncinis) and sauces on top of the meat for no extra charge. If you don't get any veggies on the bowl we don't add any extra meat or rice. As a result, the bowl can be filled halfway when no veggies are ordered.\n\nThat being said, mistakes do happen with portions, and we accept full responsibility for it. < Review>
I was on a trip from NJ to San Diego and one of my friends suggested this place. I was very hesitant to go because NJ has some of the best Shawarma places in the US. After fighting with him, I ended up going there and maaaaaan, I am so glad I went. This is hands down the top Shawarma spot for me. The crew is super friendly and awesome, the store is ridiculously clean, and it has a very modern look with a Middle Eastern touch which makes it a great atmosphere to eat in. And most importantly, the quality of the food was superb; fresh, tasty, and perfect portions of sauces and veggies with the meat and rice. I had a mixed (chicken & steak) bowl with BBQ Tahini sauce, rice and veggies and it was super scrumptious. Their freshly made pita bread is incredible. I highly recommend that place to anyone who never tried Shawarma before and those who think they've had good Shawarma before. And I was a very surprised by the price which as very affordable for this quality of the food.

I would give this place a 7 Star rating.</Review>

<review>3.5 stars. So I'm not sure why people are raving about this place. The food was good but not out of the world.

My friend and I came here on a weekday night. Cute place with decent sized seating available. You can choose a bowl or pita pocket and then add whatever else you want. She ordered the chicken shawarma pita pocket, I ordered the bowl with veggies. I don't remember which tahini sauce she took but I asked for all, which I then mixed and matched into the rice bowl. Don't get me wrong - I liked the food. But I just don't know why they have 4.5 stars on Yelp and 4.7 on Google. The bowl and pita were filling and after mixing all the sauces flavorful enough for me. And surprisingly filling considering it didn't look like a lot when we started eating.

Now the falafel was a completely different story. It's the best I've ever had! The outside was crusty and crunchy, the inside soft and tasty. With the hummus, it was a delight to have and I will come back here for it again and again.< /review>< date>

< text>
Hands down the best sandwich I've ever had. And thats saying a lot considering there are so many different types of sandwiches. Incredible and explosive flavors and so many different ingredients put into a freshly made pita (pita made in house!) that makes this the best sandwich I've ever had. As I was walking out I saw that most people were eating bowls that looked incredible, I started to regret my decision until I took the first bite lol. Which reminds me.... you know the chef has something i like to call "tastations"
Its when he/she considers every bite of the sandwich from beginning to end. And they've got it. The thing was stuffed to the rim with all the ingredients in every bite. Unlike MOST places where the first 1 0r 2 bites are all bread, the first bite was just like the middle! And the bottom of this pita pocket from heaven, ohhh the bottom! The juices the meat the pickles parsley, garlic sauce, onions, cucumbers, üçÖ,  and spices all marnenade at the bottom.... ooooweee! I had a mouthgasam. I've been to a lot of places all over the world. This places is a gem in an unlikely location. This is one of those places you'd drive an hour for.</text>

< review>
From my first visit right after they opened to now, I have been in love with this restaurant.  I have tried many items, bowls, pita's, salads, hummus, and the amazing fried cheese with fig jam.

My favorite item is the homemade warm, soft, fluffy, pita bread with the amazing garlic sauce.  Honestly I could eat that as a meal by itself (and I have).  I also love the steak shawarma salad.  I appreciate that I can add and subtract any of their fresh ingredients to make a custom salad the way I like.  I can even opt for no dressing and get a couple of their sauces to use as my dressing.  Of all the items I've tried, nothing has disappointed.  I continually crave this amazing food.

The service has never been anything but impeccable.  The employees are extremely friendly and inviting.  My order is always made perfectly, even will all of my modifications.    I have brought multiple co-workers here and it's now some of their favorite spots.  If you are looking for a wonderful, fresh, tasty meal, look no further.< /review>

<rating>4<//rating>< Review>
*Updating with an extra star since the owner reached out with a positive attitude to make it right and really values the customer experience. Looking forward to trying this place out when I'm back in San Diego again!

Upon entering, we were greeted by the friendly staff who explained our food options which were also posted up on the wall. The menu was easy to read and they offer rice bowls with salad and meat or in a freshly baked pita bread. We decided to order the Shawarma bowls since I'm not a huge steak or falafel fan. We also got a half order of the Tahini fries and Halloumi cheese sticks. For our sauces we got the garlic sauce, siracha sauce, and cilantro tahini on the side. Our food came out pretty fast within 10mins but our bowls were barely full with a handful of basmati rice hiding at the bottom with a few slices of shredded chicken added in and covered up by lots of lettuce on the top with a drizzle of sauce. There was no flavor and I found the food to be quite bland overall. Also the garlic sauce had more of a mayonnaise paste consistency rather then being saucy so just beware. The cilantro Tahini offered the most flavor out of all the sauces. The half order of fries also came out with less fries and more toppings of the olives, feta cheese and pepperonicins which was surprising since fries are usually cheaper so they should offer more instead of the toppings. My friend enjoyed the Halloumi sticks which came out with some pita bread and jam. I tried the pita bread which was freshly baked but again didn't have the tasty bread flavor to want you to keep on eating it.

I came here based on a friends recommendation and was honestly a bit disappointed. This place reminded me of the many lunch spots in NY offering mediocre Shawarma bowls. The concept is cool for a lunch spot but the flavors are just not there for me to want to come back.

Parking:
Plenty of parking available out front in the plaza and outdoor seating is available as well.</Review>

< text>
Well, that was a short lived romance...our building is around the corner from Tahini and so I told everyone I work with about this place from the second they opened. Many of us would come here 3 or 4 days a week for lunch.
The food is great and we love the concept.
But recently they had gotten busier and so they are unaccomodating with phone orders now, a bit rushed and rude on the phone, portion sizes decreased yet prices increased. I heard about this from my manager, and saw it myself today on the 3 orders before me that had bowls.

The food quality hasnt changed, its still delicious...but when I have to now pay $14 for the exact same order that I used to pay $11, and the portion is smaller, its time to say goodbye.

Coworkers are feeling the same. Thats a bummer!

My suggestion is to either to get those bowls filled up again, or bring down your prices to what they were. You have plenty of business going. But most people dont pay $14 for lunch with all the other options around the area. Being there 3 days a week for lunch was costing me $50. Maybe offer some kind of frequent customer discount or something at least, and we will return</text>

< review>
Hi everyone! Loved this place so much I had to tell you! ( and everyone I've had even minor contact with for the last 2 daysüòÖ) I went vegan a while ago so I found them using the happy cow app and they did not disappoint! They also have plenty of vegeterian options and good ol' fashioned chicken and steak dishes. I would say it's elevated middle eastern street food, and it's seriously delicious! They make the best falafel I have probably EVAH had! (seriously, break one open and smell it!) My husband tried their steak and is also in love, high quality beef, very well prepared. Their tahini is amazing and has a bunch of different flavors: reg, sriracha, bbq and more! And, most importantly, the food quality is on point; basically EVERYTHING is made from fresh ingredients in house, you name it: the falafel is made from fresh beans, no cans, powders or fillers (eggs or dairy!üòÉ); they make their own bread from scratch, and OMG can your mouth tell the difference! Their soda (both fountain and bottled) is delish, made with real sugar and comes in a lot of super tasty, interesting flavors! (Try the cherry with tarragon, you'll thank me) I have been there 3 times since finding them 2 days ago, twice on the first day! ( yeah, don't judge me until you go there!üòâ) The staff is super sweet, accommodating and helpful and you can tell how much they love their place! It is really affordable and for T- town pretty close by, soooo happy to have a great option for V food, and just plain awesome food, down the street a bit. Go there people, I need this place to stay open forever, ( tho I dont think they'll have ANY trouble) make your taste buds happy and be sure to tip the hands that feed ya üôÑ.</review>
